    * added *.exp files to gitignore (VC++ compiler output)

      (ensures that timer resolution is optimal to prevent occasional latency hitches on Win)
    * Reworded a section in SETUP.txt specific to the MQTT-LSL bridge apps
    Now multicasting can specify the local IP address to bind to. This is important if multicasting must be limited to one particular network, e.g. for a multihosted machine.
    
    There's now a "multicast.ListenAddress" property in the lsl_api.cfg file; if missing, it defaults to an empty string, which preserves the previous behavior.

    Expose streaminfo::matches_query to C API
    Replace unambiguous implementation defined int types with stdint types
    Use plain int types, include boost/cstdint.h for MSVC 2008
    Update documentation
    Add const qualifier to functions returning pugixml data that should not be changed/freed
    Mark const functions as const
    Add lsl_library_info() function to return more useful version information
    Simplify symbol export
    Added an optional time_correction prototype to return uncertainty and remote_time as well as offset.
    Normalize all the line endings
    Compile liblsl on Windows with MinGW
    
    lsl library compiles on Windows 7 with MinGW32, both for dynamic and
    static versions. Static version also compiles with Visual C++ (tested with
    Visual Studio 2015).
    Fixed warning in GCC 4.9: 'lsl::stream_info' has a field 'lsl::stream_info::obj' whose type uses the anonymous namespace 1> class stream_info {
    Added optional time-stamp post-processing to the LSL inlet. This can be used to get accurate time-synching even when the raw time stamps of a stream are heavily jittered.
    Reverting change of cboulay from Nov 4 (lsl_c.h only). Adding const (or any C++ feature) to the prototype of an extern "C" function is not advisable. This caused the exported library to have C++ name mangling rather than cdecl name mangling. The end result was the error __imp__lsl_create_streaminfo when attemping to build vs2008.sln.
    Change include files to get rid of compiler warnings that became errors using unreal build tool in Unreal Engine 4.
    Some fixes and updates here and there.
    * added *.exp files to gitignore (VC++ compiler output)
    * reverted earlier changes to SendStringMarkersC project where
      some NIDAQ code had been accidentally committed
    * fixed references to old/missing documentation in C/C++ headers.
    * added TimerResolution property to api_config / Config File
    * added code that calls timeBeginPeriod/timeEndPeriod on Windows to common.cpp
      (ensures that timer resolution is optimal to prevent occasional latency hitches on Win)
    * Reworded a section in SETUP.txt specific to the MQTT-LSL bridge apps

    Modified supergui.m and finputcheck.m to use 'handle' instead of 'real'
    for figures. This now supports the use of Figure instances in newish
    Matlab ( >= 2014b ) and the old use of floats to represent figure handles.
    This fixes #46 in upstream repo.

    Fixed GameController's release directory.
    Fixed some problems with the GameController project.
